texlive-context in Fedora 32

This page displays detailed information for a specific version of texlive-context. You might want go back to the main page of texlive-context.

Changelog

Date Author Change
2020-02-05 Than Ngo - 7:20190410-12 - fix bz#1798119 - buffer overflow in TexOpen() function, CVE-2019-19601
2020-01-31 Fedora Release Engineering - 7:20190410-11 - Rebuilt for https://fedoraproject.org/wiki/Fedora_32_Mass_Rebuild
2020-01-23 Tom Callaway - 7:20190410-10 - fix gcc10 issues
2020-01-17 Marek Kasik - 7:20190410-9 - Bring back xindy and the circular dependency on texlive-latex
2020-01-17 Marek Kasik - 7:20190410-8 - Rebuild for poppler-0.84.0 - Don't include C++ headers in C sources - Temporarily break circular dependency on texlive-latex (will be reverted)
2020-01-10 Tom Callaway - 7:20190410-7 - fix python3 issue with pdfbook2 (thanks to "Mildred", bz1733794) - fix python3 issue with latex-papersize (thanks to Silas S. Brown, bz1783964)
2019-11-15 Tom Callaway - 7:20190410-6 - package up the TL fork of psutils to help tlmgr find all the configs it expects
